    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 {'goal_states_achieved': ['on(book1,table1)'], 'game_successfully_finished': False} 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

\end{supertabular}
